manpages-dev 套件探索

下載套件

下載「manpages-dev」這個套件。

$ apt download manpages-dev

解開套件

解開「manpages-dev_4.04-2_all.deb」

$ dpkg -x manpages-dev_4.04-2_all.deb manpages-dev

觀看資料夾結構

執行

$ tree manpages-dev

顯示

下載 Source Package

執行

$ apt source manpages-dev

會下載「manpages」這個「Source Package」

套件資訊

網址: http://packages.ubuntu.com/xenial/manpages-dev

執行

$ apt show manpages-dev

顯示

Package: manpages-dev
Version: 4.04-2
Priority: optional
Section: doc
Source: manpages
Origin: Ubuntu
Maintainer: Ubuntu Developers <ubuntu-devel-discuss@lists.ubuntu.com>
Original-Maintainer: Martin Schulze <joey@debian.org>
Bugs: https://bugs.launchpad.net/ubuntu/+filebug
Installed-Size: 3,697 kB
Depends: manpages
Suggests: man-browser
Replaces: glibc-doc (<< 2.11.2-3), libaio-dev
Homepage: http://www.kernel.org/doc/man-pages/
Task: ubuntu-desktop, ubuntu-usb, kubuntu-desktop, kubuntu-full, edubuntu-desktop, edubuntu-usb, xubuntu-core, xubuntu-desktop, mythbuntu-frontend, mythbuntu-desktop, mythbuntu-backend-slave, mythbuntu-backend-master, ubuntustudio-desktop-core, ubuntustudio-desktop, ubuntu-gnome-desktop, ubuntukylin-desktop
Supported: 5y
Download-Size: 2,048 kB
APT-Manual-Installed: yes
APT-Sources: http://tw.archive.ubuntu.com/ubuntu xenial/main amd64 Packages
Description: Manual pages about using GNU/Linux for development
 These man pages describe the Linux programming interface, including
 these two sections:
  2 = Linux system calls.
  3 = Library calls (note that a more comprehensive source of information
      may be found in the glibc-doc and glibc-doc-reference packages).
